1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org

```

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching

# Grafana User Permission Model Role Coverage Audit

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in grafana/grafana that define and enforce the three-tier permission model (Viewer/Editor/Admin): the role-to-permission mapping, the permission guard middleware, and the folder/dashboard permission inheritance.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the compliance domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec.

Role Type Definition\\n\\n**`pkg/apimachinery/identity/role_type.go`** is the foundational file. It defines `RoleType` as a string, the four constants (`RoleNone`, `RoleViewer`, `RoleEditor`, `RoleAdmin`), and the `rolePrecedence` map that establishes the hierarchy (None=10, Viewer=20, Editor=30, Admin=40). The key `Includes(other RoleType) bool` method uses this precedence map to check if a role encompasses a lower role (e.g., Admin includes Editor and Viewer). `Parents()` and `Children()` methods also traverse the hierarchy.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/org/model.go`** re-exports `RoleType` and the role constants from the identity package, and defines `OrgUser` (the DB model linking a user to an org with a `RoleType` role).\\n\\n## 2. Role-to-Permission Mapping\\n\\n**`pkg/services/accesscontrol/roles.go`** defines:\\n- Constants like `BasicRolePrefix`, `FixedRolePrefix`, `RoleGrafanaAdmin`, `FixedCloudViewerRole/EditorRole/AdminRole`\\n- `BuildBasicRoleDefinitions()`: builds the basic role DTOs (basic:viewer, basic:editor, basic:admin, basic:none, basic:grafana_admin) keyed by org role string\\n- `DeclareFixedRoles(service, cfg)`: declares all OSS fixed roles and their grants to the three org roles\\n\\n**`pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/folder.go`** and **`pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/dashboard.go`** declare the `fixed:folders:viewer/editor/admin` and `fixed:dashboards:viewer/editor/admin` roles, mapping them to permission action sets and granting them to the corresponding basic org roles.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/accesscontrol/acimpl/service.go`** implements the core access control service including `DeclareFixedRoles`, `GetUserPermissions`, `getBasicRolePermissions`, and `getCachedBasicRolesPermissions`\u2014the logic that resolves what permissions a user has based on their basic role (Viewer/Editor/Admin).\\n\\n**`pkg/services/accesscontrol/database/database.go`** provides the store layer: `GetUsersBasicRoles` returns a map of userID\u2192[]string of role names (Admin, Editor, Viewer, Grafana Admin), and `GetBasicRolesPermissions` fetches all permissions assigned to the user's basic roles via the `builtin_role` table.\\n\\n## 3. Permission Guard Middleware\\n\\n**`pkg/middleware/middleware.go`** defines the pre-built middleware guards:\\n- `ReqGrafanaAdmin` \u2014 requires Grafana server admin\\n- `ReqEditorRole = RoleAuth(org.RoleEditor, org.RoleAdmin)` \u2014 allows Editor or Admin org role\\n- `ReqOrgAdmin = RoleAuth(org.RoleAdmin)` \u2014 allows only Admin org role\\n\\n**`pkg/middleware/auth.go`** implements:\\n- `RoleAuth(roles ...org.RoleType) web.Handler`: checks if `c.OrgRole` exactly matches any of the provided roles; denies if not\\n- `Auth(options *AuthOptions) web.Handler`: checks sign-in status and Grafana admin flag\\n- `CanAdminPlugins`, `RoleAppPluginAuth`: additional guards using RBAC evaluators\\n\\n**`pkg/services/accesscontrol/middleware.go`** implements the RBAC-based middleware:\\n- `Middleware(ac AccessControl) func(Evaluator) web.Handler`: wraps an RBAC `Evaluator` (e.g., `EvalPermission(\\\"dashboards:read\\\", scope)`) into a web handler that calls `ac.Evaluate()` against the signed-in user\\n- `authorize(c, ac, user, evaluator)`: injects URL params into scope templates and evaluates access\\n- `AuthorizeInOrgMiddleware`: resolves user identity in a target org before evaluating permissions\\n\\n**`pkg/services/apiserver/auth/authorizer/role.go`** implements the Kubernetes API server authorizer using org roles: Admin gets full access, Editor gets get/list/watch/create/update/patch/delete/put/post, and Viewer/None get only get/list/watch.\\n\\n**`pkg/api/accesscontrol.go`** declares all HTTP server fixed roles and their grants to org roles via `declareFixedRoles()`.\\n\\n## 4. Folder/Dashboard Permission Inheritance\\n\\n**`pkg/services/dashboards/accesscontrol.go`** is the central file for permission inheritance:\\n- Defines all action and scope constants (`ActionFoldersRead`, `ActionDashboardsWrite`, `ScopeFoldersPrefix`, etc.)\\n- `GetInheritedScopes(ctx, orgID, folderUID, folderSvc)`: walks up the folder tree via `folderSvc.GetParents()` and returns parent folder UID scopes\u2014this is how nested folder permission inheritance works\\n- `NewFolderUIDScopeResolver` and `NewFolderIDScopeResolver`: convert folder scopes into UID-based scopes including parent folder scopes\\n- `NewDashboardUIDScopeResolver` and `NewDashboardIDScopeResolver`: resolve a dashboard scope to include the dashboard's own scope, its parent folder scope, and all ancestor folder scopes\\n- `resolveDashboardScope`: calls `GetInheritedScopes` for a dashboard's folder and assembles all applicable scopes\\n\\n**`pkg/services/sqlstore/permissions/dashboard.go`** and **`pkg/services/sqlstore/permissions/dashboard_filter_no_subquery.go`** implement SQL-level permission filtering for dashboards and folders, using recursive CTEs to traverse the folder hierarchy and apply inherited permissions.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/accesscontrol/resourcepermissions/store.go`** implements `IsInherited()` to detect when a managed permission comes from a parent resource scope rather than a direct assignment.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/authz/rbac/service.go`** implements direct-DB RBAC authorization including `checkPermission` and `checkInheritedPermissions` which traverse the folder tree for permission resolution.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/authz/zanzana/translations.go`** maps Grafana's basic role names to OpenFGA relation names (`basic_viewer`, `basic_editor`, `basic_admin`, etc.) for the Zanzana authorization backend.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/user/identity.go`** and **`pkg/services/authn/identity.go`** implement `HasRole(role)` which uses `OrgRole.Includes(role)` to check if a user's role encompasses the requested role\u2014enabling the hierarchical check where Admin passes a Viewer check.\"\n}\n",

Role Type Definition\\n\\n**pkg/apimachinery/identity/role_type.go** is the foundational file. It defines `RoleType` as a string, the four constants (RoleNone, RoleViewer, RoleEditor, RoleAdmin), and the `rolePrecedence` map that establishes the hierarchy (None=10, Viewer=20, Editor=30, Admin=40). The key `Includes(other RoleType) bool` method uses this precedence map to check if a role encompasses a lower role (e.g., Admin includes Editor and Viewer). `Parents()` and `Children()` methods also traverse the hierarchy.\\n\\n**pkg/services/org/model.go** re-exports `RoleType` and the role constants from the identity package, and defines `OrgUser` (the DB model linking a user to an org with a RoleType role).\\n\\n## 2. Role-to-Permission Mapping\\n\\n**pkg/services/accesscontrol/roles.go** defines:\\n- Constants like BasicRolePrefix, FixedRolePrefix, RoleGrafanaAdmin, FixedCloudViewerRole/EditorRole/AdminRole\\n- `BuildBasicRoleDefinitions()`: builds the basic role DTOs (basic:viewer, basic:editor, basic:admin, basic:none, basic:grafana_admin) keyed by org role string\\n- `DeclareFixedRoles(service, cfg)`: declares all OSS fixed roles and their grants to the three org roles\\n\\n**pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/folder.go** and **pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/dashboard.go** declare the fixed:folders:viewer/editor/admin and fixed:dashboards:viewer/editor/admin roles, mapping them to permission action sets and granting them to the corresponding basic org roles.\\n\\n**pkg/services/accesscontrol/acimpl/service.go** implements the core access control service including DeclareFixedRoles, GetUserPermissions, getBasicRolePermissions, and getCachedBasicRolesPermissions - the logic that resolves what permissions a user has based on their basic role (Viewer/Editor/Admin).\\n\\n**pkg/services/accesscontrol/database/database.go** provides the store layer: GetUsersBasicRoles returns a map of userID to role names (Admin, Editor, Viewer, Grafana Admin), and GetBasicRolesPermissions fetches all permissions assigned to the user's basic roles via the builtin_role table.\\n\\n## 3. Permission Guard Middleware\\n\\n**pkg/middleware/middleware.go** defines the pre-built middleware guards:\\n- ReqGrafanaAdmin - requires Grafana server admin\\n- ReqEditorRole = RoleAuth(org.RoleEditor, org.RoleAdmin) - allows Editor or Admin org role\\n- ReqOrgAdmin = RoleAuth(org.RoleAdmin) - allows only Admin org role\\n\\n**pkg/middleware/auth.go** implements:\\n- `RoleAuth(roles ...org.RoleType) web.Handler`: checks if c.OrgRole exactly matches any of the provided roles; denies if not\\n- `Auth(options *AuthOptions) web.Handler`: checks sign-in status and Grafana admin flag\\n- CanAdminPlugins, RoleAppPluginAuth: additional guards using RBAC evaluators\\n\\n**pkg/services/accesscontrol/middleware.go** implements the RBAC-based middleware:\\n- `Middleware(ac AccessControl) func(Evaluator) web.Handler`: wraps an RBAC Evaluator into a web handler that calls ac.Evaluate() against the signed-in user\\n- `authorize(c, ac, user, evaluator)`: injects URL params into scope templates and evaluates access\\n- `AuthorizeInOrgMiddleware`: resolves user identity in a target org before evaluating permissions\\n\\n**pkg/services/apiserver/auth/authorizer/role.go** implements the Kubernetes API server authorizer using org roles: Admin gets full access, Editor gets get/list/watch/create/update/patch/delete/put/post, and Viewer/None get only get/list/watch.\\n\\n**pkg/api/accesscontrol.go** declares all HTTP server fixed roles and their grants to org roles via declareFixedRoles().\\n\\n## 4. Folder/Dashboard Permission Inheritance\\n\\n**pkg/services/dashboards/accesscontrol.go** is the central file for permission inheritance:\\n- Defines all action and scope constants (ActionFoldersRead, ActionDashboardsWrite, ScopeFoldersPrefix, etc.)\\n- `GetInheritedScopes(ctx, orgID, folderUID, folderSvc)`: walks up the folder tree via folderSvc.GetParents() and returns parent folder UID scopes - this is how nested folder permission inheritance works\\n- NewFolderUIDScopeResolver and NewFolderIDScopeResolver: convert folder scopes into UID-based scopes including parent folder scopes\\n- NewDashboardUIDScopeResolver and NewDashboardIDScopeResolver: resolve a dashboard scope to include the dashboard's own scope, its parent folder scope, and all ancestor folder scopes\\n- `resolveDashboardScope`: calls GetInheritedScopes for a dashboard's folder and assembles all applicable scopes\\n\\n**pkg/services/sqlstore/permissions/dashboard.go** and **pkg/services/sqlstore/permissions/dashboard_filter_no_subquery.go** implement SQL-level permission filtering for dashboards and folders, using recursive CTEs to traverse the folder hierarchy and apply inherited permissions.\\n\\n**pkg/services/accesscontrol/resourcepermissions/store.go** implements `IsInherited()` to detect when a managed permission comes from a parent resource scope rather than a direct assignment.\\n\\n**pkg/services/authz/rbac/service.go** implements direct-DB RBAC authorization including checkPermission and checkInheritedPermissions which traverse the folder tree for permission resolution.\\n\\n**pkg/services/authz/zanzana/translations.go** maps Grafana's basic role names to OpenFGA relation names (basic_viewer, basic_editor, basic_admin, etc.) for the Zanzana authorization backend.\\n\\n**pkg/services/user/identity.go** and **pkg/services/authn/identity.go** implement `HasRole(role)` which uses `OrgRole.Includes(role)` to check if a user's role encompasses the requested role - ROLE-TO-PERMISSION MAPPING\\n\\npkg/services/accesscontrol/roles.go defines BasicRolePrefix, FixedRolePrefix, RoleGrafanaAdmin, cloud role constants, BuildBasicRoleDefinitions() (builds basic role DTOs for basic:viewer/editor/admin/none/grafana_admin), and DeclareFixedRoles() (declares all OSS fixed roles and their grants to the three org roles).\\n\\npkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/folder.go and pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/dashboard.go declare fixed:folders:viewer/editor/admin and fixed:dashboards:viewer/editor/admin roles with appropriate permission action sets, granted to corresponding basic org roles.\\n\\npkg/services/accesscontrol/acimpl/service.go implements the core access control service: DeclareFixedRoles, GetUserPermissions, getBasicRolePermissions, getCachedBasicRolesPermissions - resolving user permissions based on their basic role.\\n\\npkg/services/accesscontrol/database/database.go provides GetUsersBasicRoles (maps userID to role names) and GetBasicRolesPermissions (fetches all permissions assigned to basic roles via the builtin_role table).\\n\\n3. PERMISSION GUARD MIDDLEWARE\\n\\npkg/middleware/middleware.go defines: ReqGrafanaAdmin, ReqEditorRole = RoleAuth(org.RoleEditor, org.RoleAdmin), ReqOrgAdmin = RoleAuth(org.RoleAdmin).\\n\\npkg/middleware/auth.go implements RoleAuth(roles ...org.RoleType) web.Handler (checks if c.OrgRole matches any provided role, denies if not), Auth(options) web.Handler (checks sign-in/admin status), CanAdminPlugins, and RoleAppPluginAuth.\\n\\npkg/services/accesscontrol/middleware.go implements the RBAC-based middleware: Middleware(ac AccessControl) wraps an RBAC Evaluator into a web handler calling ac.Evaluate() against the signed-in user; authorize() injects URL params into scope templates; AuthorizeInOrgMiddleware resolves user identity in a target org before evaluating.\\n\\npkg/services/apiserver/auth/authorizer/role.go implements a Kubernetes API server authorizer: Admin gets full access, Editor gets get/list/watch/create/update/patch/delete/put/post, Viewer/None get only get/list/watch.\\n\\npkg/api/accesscontrol.go declares all HTTP server fixed roles via declareFixedRoles().\\n\\n4. FOLDER/DASHBOARD PERMISSION INHERITANCE\\n\\npkg/services/dashboards/accesscontrol.go is the central inheritance file: defines all action/scope constants (ActionFoldersRead, ActionDashboardsWrite, ScopeFoldersPrefix, etc.); GetInheritedScopes() walks up the folder tree via folderSvc.GetParents() returning parent folder UID scopes; NewFolderUIDScopeResolver/NewFolderIDScopeResolver convert folder scopes to UID-based with parent scopes; NewDashboardUIDScopeResolver/NewDashboardIDScopeResolver resolve dashboard scopes including parent folder chain; resolveDashboardScope assembles all applicable scopes for a dashboard.\\n\\npkg/services/sqlstore/permissions/dashboard.go and dashboard_filter_no_subquery.go implement SQL-level permission filtering using recursive CTEs to traverse the folder hierarchy and apply inherited permissions.\\n\\npkg/services/accesscontrol/resourcepermissions/store.go implements IsInherited() to detect when a managed permission comes from a parent resource scope.\\n\\npkg/services/authz/rbac/service.go implements checkPermission and checkInheritedPermissions which traverse the folder tree for permission resolution.\\n\\npkg/services/authz/zanzana/translations.go maps basic role names to OpenFGA relation names (basic_viewer, basic_editor, basic_admin) for the Zanzana backend.\\n\\npkg/services/user/identity.go and pkg/services/authn/identity.go implement HasRole(role) using OrgRole.Includes(role) - enabling hierarchical checks where Admin passes a Viewer check.\"\n}\nJSONEOF\necho \"Done\"",
